Selected Speeches of Rev. Sun Myung Moon
442
Compiled by the Rev. Sun Myung Moon Speech Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Rev. Sun Myung Moon, who received the calling for the salvation of humanity from Heaven at the age of 16, has lived his life with a singular focus on the heavenly way! He described his life in this way:
"If Reverend Moon has any wealth, it is nothing other than the suffering I endured for public purposes rather than for myself. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. Even in the providential position, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. …… Until now, the teacher has been opposed and persecuted by the nation and the world. I was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even the Communist Party. Never in history has the world united to attack one person with the intent to eliminate him. In that sense, the teacher might be a world champion.
However, despite being cursed, I did not crumble or perish. I emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. …… Reverend Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the spirit world, hell, and even God." (Refer to Selected Speeches Vol. 105, pp. 101-103)
In a word, the life of the teacher is 'suffering itself.' The nature of this suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. Here, we come to understand who he is. The teacher is the Messiah, the Savior, and the True Parent of humanity that Christianity has hoped for over 2,000 years. Already in 185 countries worldwide, disciples following the teacher are realizing the ideal of the true family to walk the path of true children with such a confession of faith.
The teacher's identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. Issues concerning God and humans, history and the world, and the spirit world are clarified in his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled within him, setting us free. These words contain 'life.' Moreover, the more important aspect is that the teacher's words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, that is, incarnated. Therefore, life itself is the truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'the Word.'
I am confident that readers will understand the greatness of the teacher through his words. Although the realm of the teacher's words is so high and deep that it cannot be fully fathomed, it fundamentally has three characteristics.
First, through his words and life, the teacher revealed God. He liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have the bloodline of evil, they are children but cannot be called children, causing God's suffering. The teacher made the sorrowful God, who was tragically alienated due to human sin, 'speak.' He made God, who was silent and trapped within doctrines and splendidly decorated buildings, 'speak,' and made God, who could not come as the Parent of humanity, 'become the Parent,' thus the teacher is the 'complete revelation of God.'
Secondly, the teacher liberated humans from ignorance and chaos. We humans have the ability to think and make value judgments, yet we cannot deny the tragic reality that we have not fully explained our own existence. Moreover, although humans are not independent beings and are interdependent beings inseparable from others, we have not explained that relationality. The reason is that we lost God's words. Regarding this, the teacher provides the ultimate answer. Furthermore, through a life that upholds the heavenly way, he shows a concrete model path. Therefore, his words are living words overflowing with life.
Thirdly, the teacher liberated the world of all things. Every single thing created by God is an individual truth body with inherent value. Although its value should be fully realized by being under the original dominion of the original human, it was not, and thus all things lamented. Through his words, the teacher clarified the original value of the world of all things and opened the way for the liberation of all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Rev. Moon and his wife, who came as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to tirelessly give speeches worldwide, demonstrating the teachings 'Use the body of a servant with the heart of a parent' and 'Live for the sake of others' through their substantial lives, and work to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage.
Moreover, through the words of life, noble life, and achievements, the teacher has finally restored God's kingship as we enter the new millennium and has settled as the King of Blessed Families on this earth. He has been acclaimed as the King of Peace by peace activists from various fields, including politics and religion worldwide. Additionally, he has founded the Abel UN, the Universal Peace Federation, to break down the barriers of nation, race, and religion and is working tirelessly to realize the ideal of a borderless peaceful human family in 185 countries worldwide.
I hope that the readers who encounter these words will establish a true value system of life that humanity should pursue, form true families, and become key players in realizing a true peaceful world in the new millennium as owners of Cheon Il Guk. *

1)
Completion of 'Cheonnyunbawi' and Tongban Gyeokpa
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is March 7, the fourth year of Cheon Il Guk, and we stand in this place where the blessed families of heaven and earth are watching, participating in the first Sabbath morning of the new month.
With the heart of one mind, one body, one thought, and one core, through the perfection of Your creation ideal, absolute faith, absolute love, and absolute investment, we hope for the perfection of Adam and Eve's purity, pure blood, and pure love, and the settlement of the ideal of the unified world of peace that You longed for. After a long time, due to the fallen bloodline, the heart that suffered as a prisoner of the history of resentment, now the True Parents have appeared on this earth to transform everything centered on Heaven's true love, true life, and true lineage, welcoming the era of the sovereignty of God's love, the era of liberation, and the era of the heavenly fortune to liberate all nations and all things, and to establish Your homeland and the victorious liberation of Your sovereignty, we earnestly hope and wish for You to accomplish and fulfill everything at the forefront of victory with the authority to take full responsibility for everything.
Welcoming the first Sunday of the new month, we hope that everything planned for this entire month of March and this entire year will be accomplished on the foundation of Your desired hope, and that in the victorious position of the restoration of Your homeland, centered on Your ownership, everything will be completed as one world of the ideal under the sovereignty of the King of Kings, the owner of love. We earnestly hope for Your permission to make it so.
We ask that You gladly receive this worship, where all the true children of the heavenly world, saints, and all the blessed ones on this earth are united and offering devotion, and we earnestly report this in the name of the True Parents! Amen! Amen! Amen! (Entire worship, family pledge, representative prayer)
<Words> (Reading from Cheon Seong Gyeong, 'The Life of Humans and the Spirit World' section, 'Chapter 3: True Parents and the Spirit World 5) If there is only one wish left' to 'Chapter 3: Worship and Church Life Etiquette 2) Worship is the highest reverence ceremony offered to God')
The Meaning of the Song 'Cheonnyunbawi'
Stop, and sing! Teach these people how to sing. Where did you come from? "From the west." Is this your first time here? "These are the leaders from the east." Teach them the song 'Cheonnyunbawi.'
What kind of song is this? In the course of life, people can never always be smooth. There comes a time of hardship, and of course, there are various circumstances in the living environment and complications regarding those circumstances, but the greatest complication is the time of death. When one is sick, whether they recover from the illness or go to the spirit world, at such times, one must know where they stand. In a country, whether they are in the east, west, south, or center of a renowned family, they must discern their position in relation to that tradition, or problems will arise.
This song is about having a root, a foundation to avoid difficult times in one's life. Therefore, although it is a popular song, I instructed that it be included in the hymnal. When you listen to its content, you will realize there is deep meaning, and you should learn this song, thinking of it as a song that can defend against difficulties in your path, if you have a united heart. Sing it once. (Song 'Cheonnyunbawi')
The reason for incorporating 'Cheonnyunbawi' into the hymnal
At the end, after completing Tongban Gyeokpa and completely organizing Satan's bloodline, the song that declares one will go directly to the heavenly kingdom from the position of the owner is so significant. Even the thousand-year-old rock longs for and follows the example.
Now, everyone, even those who are here for the first time, sing along. The meaning is profound. The eastern sky refers to Korea, where the Lord resides, and in the face of the passing years, the thousand-year-old rock standing at the crossroads is like the king of the post, guarding the unchanging outpost to eliminate Satan's bloodline from this earth, and can stand in the position of the owner wherever Heaven goes! Amen! You should think like this. Sing along. (Song 'Cheonnyunbawi') (Prayer by Assistant Jeong Won Ju) (Worship) *

Proclamation of the Inheritance of the Three Great Kingships
Today is an important day, March 8, the fourth year of Cheon Il Guk. Therefore, starting with the letter from God to the teacher, followed by the resolution proclaimed by the four great saints and the leaders of the five major religions! Since such a new resolution has been proclaimed, we must open up everything that has been blocked in the spirit world until now. You should know that.
The significance of 8 o'clock on March 8, the fourth year of Cheon Il Guk, and the special proclamation prayer
The time has come for the Heavenly Parent, the Parent of Heaven and Earth, and the Parent of Heaven, Earth, and Humankind to land on this earth. Therefore, at 8 o'clock on March 8, the fourth year of Cheon Il Guk, 3 times 8 is 24 (3×8=24), I will pray for you. Until then, we will conduct a Hoon Dok Hae session.
In regard to the resolution adopted by all the ancestors in history, we must connect it to the earth, establish sibling relationships, and establish sister relationships centered on the east, west, south, and north. We must bind everything that is scattered. Bind it east and west, bind it north and south, and bind all 360 degrees together with the spirit world and the earthly world.
By doing so, God can come to the earth freely and work centered on the spirit world. Then, centered on Korea, Japan, and the United States, we must also bind them together. Just as we conducted cross-cultural marriages, we must establish cross-cultural sibling ties, cross-national ties, and cross-world ties to completely open up this day.
We must pray for this so that everything we do flows in one vein. We must bind it together. Therefore, the Parents prepared anew this morning, made a promise, and attended this place, knowing this, and we must conduct the Hoon Dok Hae with such a heart. Do you understand? "Yes."
Park Jeong Min, are you here? Start with the resolution. Then, centered on the five major religions, the resolution of the four great saints, and then the resolution of the communist bloc, in that order? "Yes." Then the resolution of the world's journalists, followed by the resolution of the President of the United States! Continue on, then the resolution of the kings of the Goryeo and Joseon dynasties in Korea! All the resolutions they adopted after being educated!
Now, centered on Goguryeo, we must bind the historical enmity with China. We must proclaim that it has entered the direct management authority of God.
Therefore, on March 8, the fourth year of Cheon Il Guk, at 8 o'clock, 3 times 8 is 24 (3×8=24), and 4 times 8 is 32 (4×8=32). With the number 8 appearing four times, adding the 4 years makes it 36, the number of liberation and completion.
Because it is such an important day, the Parents prepared yesterday, and therefore, centered on the group of blessed families and others, the Parents have come with the conditions to make the final declaration and decision. You should know that.
Now, knowing this, we will start the Hoon Dok Hae. We will continue until 8 o'clock. Where are you from this time? "From the southern part of Seoul." Where in the south? "Yeongdeungpo…." Does it include Heukseok-dong? "Gwanak, Yangcheon, Guro, Geumcheon, Dongjak." Who is the leader there? "Here." Okay. Let's begin!
Do not be ashamed before the saints and sages of the spirit world
"This is the letter from God to the True Parents." Do not think of it as a letter only to the teacher, but as a message to everyone centered on the Heavenly Parent, the Parent of Heaven and Earth, and the Parent of Heaven, Earth, and Humankind. Listen with that mindset. Go ahead! (Reading from "God is the Parent of Humanity")
『……The Divine Principle gives us new hope, and its content is clear. God did not create us in a complicated way. God instructed us in only one direction of the way. However, after being trapped in the firmament for a long time, now Gautama seems to have been reorganized and recreated into a new human form.』
Is the president of the Segye Ilbo here? "Yes." Publish this again in the Segye Ilbo. Do you understand? "We have already published this content." Publish it again. You published it separately. Publish it comprehensively! March 8 is important. 'Although the entire spirit world has come out divided like this, now it has equipped a unified direction, and it is time to apply this to the ethnic, national, and global fields, so we are publishing it anew comprehensively.' Make it clear and publish it. Do you understand? "Yes."
Even publishing up to here is fine, the part about the five major religions. Then stop, and then continue as a series, 1st, 2nd, 3rd, and compile it into a book to sell and introduce to the public. Since it was published in the newspaper, a passing newspaper that not everyone may have paid attention to, you must make it so that anyone can take an interest. Do you understand? "Yes." Understand clearly.
Today is the 8th. When will you publish it? "I will prepare it right away." By what date? By the 10th, the founding day of the Universal Peace Federation! Along with the commemoration of the founding of the Family Party, include an introduction about how the spirit world has come out, and conclude by stating that we will continue to publish such series of content in 1st, 2nd, and 3rd parts. Do you understand? "Yes." Publishing it in 1, 2, 3, 4 series will be quite significant. The series published should be compiled into a single book and sold on the market and disclosed worldwide.
What you must know is this: when you go to the spirit world, you must not be ashamed before the saints and sages who have testified to these facts, and you must not be ashamed when you meet Jesus, Confucius, Buddha, or Muhammad.
All these saints and sages who have participated and testified here will not die. They will live eternally in the spirit world and strive to realize the content of these facts along with history. Therefore, they will inevitably appear in history. Therefore, in representing the spirit world and the earthly world, the path of life you walk must match that, and you must think seriously about how you will cross such a position.
Now is the time when the Parent of Heaven, Earth, and Humankind can directly manage
Understanding this principle and knowing this content, you must prepare a foundation to deal with it. Therefore, today, March 8, the fourth year of Cheon Il Guk, 3 times 8 is 24 (3×8=24), 4 times 8 is 32 (4×8=32), adding the number 4 makes 36! In the I Ching, 36 represents flying. It signifies the end. Therefore, the teacher must clarify this on earth so that the spirit world can abandon factional lines and move toward a unified direction.
Why? God is leading. Jesus is leading, and then the Parent of Heaven, Earth, and Humankind is leading. Until now, God has appeared in the spirit world as an intangible being, but now, the Parent of Heaven, Earth, and Humankind must connect with the era where they can directly manage with the form of the true parent that all religious groups have longed for but have not seen the ideal fruit. Only then can the earthly world stand at the final destination of the peaceful world.
Therefore, organizing this content and establishing it as a central theme is an extremely historical and providential demand, and you must not become a person ashamed before this will. You must realize this and go forward.
You must not live recklessly. Women must not live recklessly, men must not live recklessly, families must not live recklessly, and nations must not live recklessly. What is this country? We must clean up the likes of stray dogs. It cannot remain unorganized. No matter how much they make a fuss, the spirit world will bring God to the forefront, and all the leaders under the saints and sages will go to the representatives of atheists and plant them upside down.
Since everything has been prepared, by connecting to the path of victory in the practice course, the path of the ideal of creation and love, you can be grafted into eternal life and survival. You must awaken to this yourself. Do you understand? "Yes."
Even communists are God's children, so we must open the way for them
Now, the next! "Next is the representative of the communist bloc." The representatives of the communist bloc, these stray dogs! They were supposed to be thrown into hell, but by blessing the saints and murderers, we have built a bridge for them to repent their wrongdoings before God.
You need to know that they were called not because they were great, but because they were centered on the teacher's merit and under the teacher's special command! Because within the teacher's words there are principles and intentions to return the satanic world to its original position, they were granted special privileges to solve the content of those words, just as murderers were blessed and placed in positions of representation. In the religious field, enemies and ideological enemies were newly established to fill the gaps in their fields in this new era's framework.

Originally, these people wouldn't even be able to attend or witness the place where such letters are announced, where the resolutions of the five great saints are announced. The fact that they were liberated and established to announce resolutions in the communist sphere is not an easy task. You must know how difficult it was to achieve this. From now on, you must understand and accept all declarations that have been made from this perspective. Do you understand? "Yes." Now!

Proclamation of the Inheritance of the Three Great Kingships

『...Marx acknowledges God and has come to this place to testify that God is the parent of all humanity. I, Marx, confidently declared on earth to deny God and believe in me more than God. From now on, I want to publicly reveal my experiences with God to the whole world. I first met Mr. Lee Sang-heon here in the spiritual world and had several conversations from an ideological perspective, hearing truly amazing content and being greatly fascinated.』

Now, if the communists come to know this, and if they go to the other world and say, 'Even after such announcements, did you persist with communist ideology?' where would they go? They would become wandering stars. They have no hometown and no place to be. Whether it's the Soviet Union, China, North Korea, or South Korea, they become wanderers because they are like people without heads. As they wander, they might be sucked into the dark world of the infinite universe—there's a term called a black hole—and disappear.

Even those people were born with the ties of brothers as God's children, so the True Parents have the responsibility to open the way for them as well, and they are opening the way. Despite this, they must participate here, where all saints and sages have adopted resolutions in the era of heavenly liberation under the responsibility and consensus of their leaders. They must proclaim this with amazement and gratitude.

Now, the time has come when people like Marx and Stalin, those brutal individuals, can come to earth and beat and chase people with clubs, doing all sorts of things. It's a time when blessings and diseases can be given. The time has come when the spiritual world will deal with things mercilessly.

Your ancestors are the same. They give blessings and diseases to their descendants. In order to match this astonishing reality, if a disease has occurred, in surgery, if it's an arm, the arm must be cut, and if it's a leg, the leg must be cut. Even if they are placed in the junkyard of the spiritual world, the ancestors have the responsibility to quickly cut off what can lead their descendants to ruin and defend against it. You must know that there is a responsibility of your bloodline. You must know that the time has come to deal with the earth mercilessly. Do you understand? "Yes."

When your brother knows that fact, if the brother is within that factual realm, it must be dealt with quickly if he's a patient. In surgery, when the eye is to be removed, it must be removed, and when the nose is to be cut, it must be cut. Even if he remains as a cripple forever in the other world, remaining as a cripple is not the problem. Since it affects future generations and descendants, the germs must be removed, and it must be dealt with cleanly in the spiritual world, so unimaginable tragedies will occur in the world. People who are not thinking will die suddenly.

Especially, with traffic accidents or diseases like AIDS, they will be cleaned up like fallen leaves in autumn without the general public knowing. God also wants this, and the Parents of Heaven, Earth, and Humankind want this, so you must know that they have stepped into the arena to clean this up. Therefore, by gathering all together, a conclusive page is made to create a new book, entering the era after the cosmic revolution. Amen! Say Amen. "Amen!"

Now, you must wear glasses and go centered on the standard that the saints and sages see. Only then can you, who live on earth with the True Parents, know that you are the great elder, the great king, and the great king's grandchild. You must become the model. Do you understand or not? "I understand!"

From now on, you must shake your head, and if you know the facts of the spiritual world, you must go through a tunnel process that you must break through. If it's the sea, you must navigate the sea, and if it's the spiritual world, you must know everything in the intangible world and receive guidance from the teacher on the compass of your specialty, your country, the world, and the spiritual world. You must know that there is no way out unless you follow the path the teacher takes.

It's not a joke. Do you understand? "Yes." You, who are here, must become the resurrected bodies of those who disappeared in the struggle of good and evil. How many people disappeared in misfortune, whether they were evil or good? Standing in such a position is to save them all. You must live on earth in the position of the resurrected body, the elder brother's position, the royal son's position, and the substitute position of the Parents of Heaven and Earth.

If you do not share the awareness that you must go in a leading position toward that goal, you will have a life of resentment that can be accused hundreds or thousands of times more than the saints and sages lamenting in the future world. Why? How precious is the earthly life serving the True Parents? Do you understand or not? "I understand!"

You must know yourself as someone like a kindergartener who knows nothing, and do not wag your tail and shake your head. You must accept this and know it, and then you must reawaken yourself. The time is urging you to do so. For that time, the teacher must proclaim this today. If you establish the law, you must proclaim it, right? "Yes."

You must be able to be respected in the earthly world and the spiritual world

Just as it is proclaimed in the name of the president of a country, standing in the historical representative position of the Parents of Heaven and Earth, you must proclaim this so that the proclamation opens the way to the eternal world of all nations, not just all directions. Since that world enters the direct dominion of goodness, anyone must accept the content of the proclamation with absolute obedience, absolute love, and absolute faith. Do you understand or not? "I understand!"

You must know how much you have acted wickedly, thinking lightly of the teacher and saying, 'What about the Unification Church?' while coming out until now, wondering whether to believe the teacher's words or not. Do you think the teacher would think of God that way? You must also know the fact that the teacher could not help but live worrying about providing a model that they could follow on earth to save them, knowing how the saints should live.

Therefore, living according to such content under the direct command of the True Parents, whom the entire spiritual world pays attention to, you must be able to be respected in the earthly world and the spiritual world as a living being with the five senses and six senses moving. If you cannot be respected, you become a dung dog, and the teacher will kick you away with his foot. Just like kicking a soccer ball over the fence on the ground, he will kick you away.

You must make a new resolution from today not to become such a pitiful person. You must accept this word with the meaning of awakening and make a new resolution to become a filial family in front of Cheon Il Guk, a loyal family, and a family of saints and holy sons. You must know that you cannot avoid making such a resolution. You must act in this place, where you must trample on and kick away all organizations and whatnot. If you have the authority of a president, you can overturn that country in an instant overnight and register it in the heavenly kingdom.

Isn't that right? If the leader of the Grand National Party declares in the National Assembly that the Grand National Party has joined the Democratic Party at once, should you follow or not? If the leader of the Democratic Party declares joining the Grand National Party, you must follow, and what is the name of the Open Party? "Open Our Party." What 'our' comes to mind when you say 'our'? Is it a new pen, a pig pen? (Laughter)

Do they have the qualification to say 'our'? Is there a concept of 'our' in the communist world? When they become political enemies, they purge them. My goodness! You don't know communism, but I know communism well, so I established the Victory Over Communism ideology. I have been tortured a lot in front of them, imprisoned, and learned all sorts of miraculous content, so I did it to uproot it with my own hands.

The Unification Church, which possesses the terrifying bomb of truth

I am the one who ordered Gorbachev to take down the statues of Marx and Lenin. The same goes for Kim Jong-il of North Korea. When he asked his father, 'Oh my, how can we achieve national unification if you die?' he said, 'Follow Reverend Moon.' I am the one who received such secret notifications three times. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

With leftist ideology, as a liberal young party person, try doing it your way. If frost falls overnight, will the young radishes and cabbages survive? When snow falls, the young ones run away at once. Our Unification Church, if we legally gather thousands of people in a place like the United States and educate them, they will all become like vegetables within a week.

The terrifying bomb of truth that the Unification Church possesses, armed with truth, is not a problem of an atomic bomb. The world has trampled on this, and they have treated Reverend Moon, the main figure, as the worst person, doing all sorts of things. Even the Unification Church itself, influenced by that, has a fact of falling like autumn leaves in a position where it could deny. Now, since it is the time of liberation, everyone is saying, 'Oh, oh, good!' but you cannot just step into a position where you can be good.

If you do not stand in the position of the elder brother, the father's position, and the king's position, which can guide the saints and sages, you cannot guide the people of the spirit world who were kings, fathers, and brothers. Do you understand or not? "I understand!" Raise your hand if you understand. You raise your hands well. Put them down!

Now, when the teacher sees you, he will glare at you. If he tries to curse, his tongue will be twisted. If he curses, he will be caught immediately. Therefore, you must think about finding a way to avoid living with you.

There is no one to welcome you when you meet. Think about it.

You are fighting with your body and mind, right? "Yes." One, two, three, four, that gentleman has come. Are your body and mind fighting or not? "They are fighting." How do they fight? You want to do as your body desires, right? I'm asking you. "No." Then? Do you win over the world of the mind, or does the world of the body win?

In the end, the mind surrenders. Why? The body experienced love first. The body is where Satan grafted the love of the growing stage of God's lineage. The world of the mind is different. It was growing without knowing the love of the future that could grow 33 percent more. Therefore, the body received Satan's blood. The world of the mind did not receive God's blood. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, in the end, the body does as it pleases. Everything has become individualistic. It has become individualistic, and what is it? Men and women have become animals, worse than animals. These things, regardless of anyone, beyond the country, if there is a beauty, they want to make it theirs, and if there is a handsome man, they want to make it theirs, so what should I say, they have all become wolves. Men and women, their eyes and all five senses are all like that.

Therefore, what Satan desires is free sex! What kind of sexual liberation? If sexual liberation is achieved, if there is an owner who has achieved sexual liberation, it means that any woman, whether mother, grandmother, queen, or any woman in the world, is mine. It means that you can swim and go anywhere. My goodness! Where is the order like that? Did you evolve from an amoeba to become a person?

The principle of species is that only when male and female love each other can something better than themselves, their children, be born. Countless... Even amoebas have male and female counterparts. Today, it is said that even in the world of germs, there are males and females that give birth to offspring. So, if they give birth to offspring, can they find a result that can change more than their children by following the steps of love? You cannot ignore the principle of species.

Therefore, the many countries that have emerged are what? They were driven out centered on their ancestors, holding grudges and emerging like factions, and that's how it has become. You cannot overcome that. If you had evolved from an amoeba, you would become princes of peace and unity, but you cannot. They go into the trash can.

What, young people demonstrate and say they will take power? Try taking it. See how many days it lasts. If it is decided in the world's parliament and I educate them, they will all collapse within a week. They cannot withstand it theoretically. 'Answer me!' These bastards, like gourds with strings cut off, do you think they can go around as they please when the wind blows? If you kick them, they will all break and disappear. Do you understand? "Yes."

The relationship between father and son and destiny

I am preparing for that now. The time is almost here. Even if I am not here, I have taught you everything you need to establish a nation, right? Have I taught you, or not? "You have taught us." Kwak Jeong-hwan! "Yes." Can you become the owner of the country? I'm asking you. "Yes." Again! "Yes." Again! "Yes, I will." Again! "Yes." You bastards, again! "Yes." Again! "Yes." Again! "Yes." Jeong Dae-hwa! "Yes."

You must do it. You must have a new awakening. When you are called before God and the resolutions of the saints and sages, and you are questioned about your responsibility, you cannot help but say 'Yes' when you are a son and a prince. Do you understand? "Yes." Knowing that he is the father and knowing that he is the son.

It is the bloodline that connects the love of parents and the life of parents. If the bloodline is not connected, the relationship between father and son does not emerge. The relationship between father and son cannot become a fateful task. Can you buy a father with money? "No." Can you buy a mother with money? "No." Not even with heaven and earth. Even God cannot help it. There is a word for fate and destiny. Fate is the heavenly way. They do not know the fateful task of human ethics and morality. They have come to know the fateful task of human ethics and morality through Reverend Moon.

What's the husband's name? "Yoo Jung-ok." Yoo Jung-ok sounds like a woman's name, but he was a man. So he thinks he got a wife who sings well. Is he here? I saw the father over there. "Do it together. (Mother)" Ah, sing and do it. Singing is for women, it doesn't suit men. Yes. (Cho Myung-won sings) (During the song) Groom, come out and help a bit.

Applause! (Applause) Father applause, mother applause, son applause! It's a family that sings, so today we should honor them as a musical family. Father, come out too. "Since the bride is here, come out together...." Yes, did you come? Let's see. Yes! That daughter-in-law, I sent her to the Yoo family, and I feel cool in my heart, should I say? Now that you've got a good eldest daughter-in-law, you'll owe her a lot. "Yes." You shouldn't just stand like a man and say good things, now you should look at your wife and live with respect for the earth, and happiness will come. Try it once. It's good for a daughter-in-law to do this with her father-in-law. Applause! (Applause)

Mother worked hard to pair them up this time. You don't know how hard Mother worked. "Tell the in-laws to come out too." If the in-laws are here, the in-laws should come out. (Laughter) Are they here? Is the groom not here? "He came in the morning." Not here? This lady.... Didn't the thirty-five-year-old bride get married? "Yes. (Lee Won-dae)" Where did she go? "She went to school." School? "Yes." A woman trying to become a doctor will get smashed.
What song do you want to sing? (Song for the family of Chairman Yoo Jeong-ok) Let's have the father-in-law teach a representative song and sing it all at once. Everyone knows it, right? Let's start. "What song?" You know the one you do, right? (Yoo Jeong-ok's song) The strength of the Unification Church comes from the family.

Kang Jeong-ja! Bring your husband out. "We had a 70th birthday gathering with the family last time, and my son hosted it, my eldest son Yeong-san. He said that everyone knows my father is tone-deaf, so please understand and made him sing. It was a very fun atmosphere. (Yoo Jong-gwan)" Really? Couples match well. (Laughter) Who is better looking? Is the woman better looking, or the man? The man is better looking, right? "Yes, the man is better looking." "They look alike." (Yoo Jong-young-Kang Jeong-ja song)

Gwak Jeong-hwan! Yoon Jeong-eun! Try to have fun. "I used to sing well, but I got sick in the middle and forgot the lyrics...." You were good at singing and writing poetry. (Gwak Jeong-hwan-Yoon Jeong-eun song)

This time, our hometown in Pyeongan-do, Shin Dong-chun? "Yes." What Chun is it? "Shin Dong-chun." "May I say a word.... (Yoon Jeong-eun)" No more words, just sing. Shin Dong-chun! You're the wind-catching lady, so you're allowed to talk briefly about your travels from the Soviet Union. Try talking once. It's the first time seeing this lady, right? Many people might not know her. Give her a round of applause. "Oh no." What's the big deal? "Thank you for remembering." Don't tell me not to. You don't want to see my face. (Shin Dong-chun professor's testimony and report)

"......How can you say such big words when you haven't sung together often? And even when singing alone, you should hold that slender waist tightly and sing...." You should hug tightly and kiss a bit, why didn't you? (Laughter) "Father likes kissing too much...." Oh my! That's a big deal. Such a big deal, this. (Laughter) (Song)

Who came as a couple next? Moon Sang-hee! Did your husband come? "He didn't come." Why didn't you bring him? "We came as a couple. (Park Joong-hyun)" As a couple. Choi? "Choi Hyun-sook." Hyun-sook! Boast a bit about your bride. Are you serving your grandfather? "Yes." (Park Joong-hyun chairman's testimony)

"......Here, Chairman Moon Nan-young is my aunt." Is she your aunt? "Yes, she's my paternal aunt. She's a year older than me, but we're fifth cousins." That family does everything. (Laughter) "Chairman Moon Nan-young came to our family as a daughter-in-law, and my grandfather loved Chairman Moon Nan-young. He often sent letters to Chairman Moon Nan-young while he was alive, saying he was grateful for sending such a great woman as a daughter-in-law. If you read those letters now, they're such masterpieces.... 'To my beloved niece-in-law.'" My beloved daughter-in-law whom I want to put into my bones!

Is he your grandson? "So she's my niece-in-law." Then he's your uncle here. "My grandfather is my uncle." "My grandfather is my great-uncle. (Park No-hee)" So he's your uncle here. "I'm a fifth cousin." He's your paternal uncle. "When I personally meet Chairman Moon Nan-young, even though she's a year older aunt, I bow deeply." Try doing it once together. (Laughter) Do it. Receive blessings. (Park Joong-hyun chairman bows deeply to Chairman Moon Nan-young) (Applause) In Confucian thought, it is said 'A harmonious family is the foundation of all success,' meaning receiving blessings. That's how everyone lives. Indeed. (Testimony continues)

"......I received an honorary doctorate from the Christian Leadership Seminary in Boston, Massachusetts. It was given by the established church seminary. They volunteered to give it. This is the glory that True Parents nurtured, but I have always been lacking, so I couldn't report it to the Parents. I take this opportunity to mention it today." Give another round of applause. (Applause) (Park Joong-hyun-Choi Hyun-sook song)

Yoo Jong-gwan! "Yes." Who is your bride? Park, right? "Yes." Bring her and talk a bit and sing. Talk about how you live. We need a model testimony of the family. You need to know that the foundation of the Unification Church's strength is in that family.

Tell your mother to come out soon. Now, you need to prepare to separate and go to America, finish everything, and then go. Contact your mother. Contact your mother.

Tell her to come out. Come out. Talk a bit about how you live as a couple. "Park Young-ja, come here." (Laughter) (Yoo Jong-gwan chairman's testimony)

"......I haven't treated her like a queen and she has always lived in my shadow without a name or light. She's still living like that, but from now on, I don't know how long I can maintain it, but from this moment on, I will serve her well."

To treat her like a queen, the teacher needs to provide money, that's what it means. (Laughter) "I will repent and do as Father does for Mother." (Applause)

It's now nine o'clock, and soon it will be ten, eleven, and then twelve, and it seems like we should leave. "But when do you have breakfast? At twelve? (Mother)" Well, if we finish at nine.... "If we finish now, until twelve?" No. Finish, do everything, and when it's time to leave by twelve, eat, go to the bathroom, and these people who came to say goodbye in tears should part with a joyful song at the end, because that's the most tactful farewell, so I asked Mother to come out. Sorry. You should sing once. You two sing well. You did well yesterday too. (Yoo Jong-gwan-Park Young-ja song)

Wonju! Come down and sing 'Thousand-Year Rock,' and let's finish together! (Chorus of 'Thousand-Year Rock.' Father and Mother sing) Let's pray briefly. (The prayer content was not recorded due to poor recording quality) (Bow)

'Heavenly Mother, Earthly Mother' Pray with a heart that loves Mother. So, the era of women's liberation has opened, and now from Korea, start a women's movement, blossom, and connect with North and South Korea, China, and the United States, pray and devote yourself, and continue such practical movements. It has started. You know, right? "Yes." (Applause) *
